ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {

ghost function MaxOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y
          // Both x==m and y==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
          assert m == x; // since x==y and x is the maximum value
          assert cnt >= 2; // both x and y counted
          assert false; // contradiction
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
          assert m == x; // since x==z and x is the maximum value
          assert cnt >= 2; // both x and z counted
          assert false; // contradiction
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
          assert m == y; // since y==z and y is the maximum value
          assert cnt >= 2; // both y and z counted
          assert false; // contradiction
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)

  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {

    b := if x <= z then x else z;

    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;

    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;

  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }

  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)

  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y
          // Both x==m and y==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y
          assert MaxOf(b', c') <= a';
          assert m == a' == x;
          // Both x==m and y==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert x == m;
          assert y == m;
          assert cnt >= 2;
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
          // y = MaxOf(a',c') <= b' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = z
          assert MaxOf(a', c') <= b';
          assert m == b' == x;
          // Both x==m and z==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert x == m;
          assert z == m;
          assert cnt >= 2;
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
          // x = MaxOf(a',b') <= c' = y, so m = max(x,y,z) = y = z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') <= c';
          assert m == c' == y;
          // Both y==m and z==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert y == m;
          assert z == m;
          assert cnt >= 2;
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;
  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int

        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y

ghost function MaxOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 &&
         MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z
      {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
          // Since a' is largest, z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x
          assert z <= a';
          // m = max(x, y, z) = a' = x = y, and x == m
          assert m == x;
          // cnt counts how many of x, y, z equal m; here both x and y equal m
          assert cnt >= 2;
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
          // Since b' is largest, y = MaxOf(a',c') <= b' = x
          assert y <= b';
          // m = max(x, y, z) = b' = x = z, and x == m
          assert m == x;
          // cnt counts how many of x, y, z equal m; here both x and z equal m
          assert cnt >= 2;
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
          // Since c' is largest, x = MaxOf(a',b') <= c' = y
          assert x <= c';
          // m = max(x, y, z) = c' = y = z, and y == m
          assert m == y;
          // cnt counts how many of x, y, z equal m; here both y and z equal m
          assert cnt >= 2;
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

  if a < b then a else b

ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;
  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      // We prove that no positive a',b',c' can satisfy all three equations
      // when cnt < 2.  We do it by contradiction: assume such a',b',c' exist.
      assume a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 &&
            MaxOf(a', b') == x &&
            MaxOf(a', c') == y &&
            MaxOf(b', c') == z;
      // Determine which variable is the largest among a',b',c'.
      if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
        // a' is the maximum
        assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
        assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
        assert x == a' && y == a';
        // a' > b' and a' > c' implies x > z ? Actually z <= a'.
        assert z <= a';
        // Since x == y == a', both x and y equal the maximum m.
        assert x == m;
        assert y == m;
        // cnt counts how many of x,y,z equal m.
        assert cnt >= 2;
      } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
        // b' is the maximum
        assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
        assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
        assert x == b' && z == b';
        // Since b' is largest, x == z == b'.
        assert x == z;
        assert m == x; // m is the overall max of x,y,z
        // x==z==m, so cnt counts at least two of them.
        assert cnt >= 2;
      } else {
        // c' is the maximum
        assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
        assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
        assert y == c' && z == c';
        // Since c' is largest, y == z == c'.
        assert y == z;
        assert m == y; // m is the overall max of x,y,z
        // y==z==m, so cnt >= 2.
        assert cnt >= 2;
      }
      // Contradiction: cnt >= 2 but we are in the branch where cnt < 2.
      assert false;
    }
  }
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')

          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y

  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
          // Since a' >= b' and a' >= c', we have a' = max(a',b') = max(a',c')
          // Thus m = max(x,y,z) = a' and both x and y equal m
          assert m == a';
          assert x == m && y == m;
          // This contradicts cnt == 1, so this case cannot happen.
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
          // Since b' >= a' and b' >= c', we have b' = max(a',b') = max(b',c')
          // Thus m = max(x,y,z) = b' and both x and z equal m
          assert m == b';
          assert x == m && z == m;
          // This contradicts cnt == 1, so this case cannot happen.
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z

          assert m == c';
          assert y == m && z == m;
          // This contradicts cnt == 1, so this case cannot happen.
        }
      }
    }
  }

ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;
  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {

        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y

          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }

    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.

          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';

  if z > m { m := z; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;

  } else {

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;
  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')

      exists c ::

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)

        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y

ghost function MaxOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
          // Since a' >= c', MaxOf(b', c') <= a', so z <= a', thus m = a' = x = y
          assert MaxOf(b', c') <= a';
          assert z <= a';
          assert m == a'; // m is the maximum of x,y,z
          assert x == m && y == m;
          // Therefore both x and y equal m, hence cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert cnt >= 2;
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
          // Since b' >= a', MaxOf(a', c') <= b', so y <= b', thus m = b' = x = z
          assert MaxOf(a', c') <= b';
          assert y <= b';
          assert m == b'; // m is the maximum of x,y,z
          assert x == m && z == m;
          // Therefore both x and z equal m, hence cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert cnt >= 2;
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
          // Since c' >= a', MaxOf(a', b') <= c', so x <= c', thus m = c' = y = z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') <= c';
          assert x <= c';
          assert m == c'; // m is the maximum of x,y,z
          assert y == m && z == m;
          // Therefore both y and z equal m, hence cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert cnt >= 2;
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;
  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y
          // Both x==m and y==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

  if a > b then a else b

  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y
          // Both x==m and y==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }

ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

ghost function MaxOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
